Civmec,2017-7,Moving Average Price (n periods): Sum of Prices for each Period/Number of Periods
Civmec,2017-7,Price Close/Moving Avg Price: Latest Price/Moving Average Price
Civmec,2017-7,Price/NTA: Closing Share Price/Net Tangible Assets Per Share (times)
Civmec,2017-7,Relative Price Change [RPC]: Relative price change is price change of stock with respect to Benchmark Index
Civmec,2017-7,"Relative Strength (6 Months): Price close today/Price close 6 months ago, then ranked by percentile within the entire market."
Civmec,2017-7,TSR: Total Shareholder Returns is expressed as an annualized rate of return for shareholders after allowing for capital appreciation and dividend
Civmec,2017-7,Volume Index (VI): Number of shares traded in the period/Average number of shares traded for the period
Civmec,2017-7,Volume Weighted Average Price (VWAP): The Volume Weighted Average Price (VWAP) is the summation of turnover divided by total volume in the same period.

Civmec,2017-7,Annual Return: Dividends Paid In a 12-Month Period/Price at the Beginning of the Period + Capital Gain or Loss over 1 Year/Price 1 Year Ago (%)
Civmec,2017-7,Moving Average Price (n periods): Sum of Prices for each Period/Number of Periods
Civmec,2017-7,Price Close/Moving Avg Price: Latest Price/Moving Average Price
Civmec,2017-7,Price/NTA: Closing Share Price/Net Tangible Assets Per Share (times)
Civmec,2017-7,Relative Price Change [RPC]: Relative price change is price change of stock with respect to Benchmark Index
Civmec,2017-7,"Relative Strength (6 Months): Price close today/Price close 6 months ago, then ranked by percentile within the entire market."
Civmec,2017-7,TSR: Total Shareholder Returns is expressed as an annualized rate of return for shareholders after allowing for capital appreciation and dividend
Civmec,2017-7,Volume Index (VI): Number of shares traded in the period/Average number of shares traded for the period
Civmec,2017-7,Volume Weighted Average Price (VWAP): The Volume Weighted Average Price (VWAP) is the summation of turnover divided by total volume in the same period.
Civmec,2017-7,"Data for the BuySellSignals algorithms is drawn from annual reports, company websites and similar sources of publicly available data. It should be used as a guide only."

Civmec,2017-7,Annual Return: Dividends Paid In a 12-Month Period/Price at the Beginning of the Period + Capital Gain or Loss over 1 Year/Price 1 Year Ago (%)
Civmec,2017-7,Moving Average Price (n periods): Sum of Prices for each Period/Number of Periods
Civmec,2017-7,Price Close/Moving Avg Price: Latest Price/Moving Average Price
Civmec,2017-7,Price/NTA: Closing Share Price/Net Tangible Assets Per Share (times)
Civmec,2017-7,Relative Price Change [RPC]: Relative price change is price change of stock with respect to Benchmark Index
Civmec,2017-7,"Relative Strength (6 Months): Price close today/Price close 6 months ago, then ranked by percentile within the entire market."
Civmec,2017-7,TSR: Total Shareholder Returns is expressed as an annualized rate of return for shareholders after allowing for capital appreciation and dividend
Civmec,2017-7,Volume Index (VI): Number of shares traded in the period/Average number of shares traded for the period
Civmec,2017-7,Volume Weighted Average Price (VWAP): The Volume Weighted Average Price (VWAP) is the summation of turnover divided by total volume in the same period.
Civmec,2017-7,"Data for the BuySellSignals algorithms is drawn from annual reports, company websites and similar sources of publicly available data. It should be used as a guide only."

Civmec,2017-7,Annual Return: Dividends Paid In a 12-Month Period/Price at the Beginning of the Period + Capital Gain or Loss over 1 Year/Price 1 Year Ago (%)
Civmec,2017-7,Moving Average Price (n periods): Sum of Prices for each Period/Number of Periods
Civmec,2017-7,Price Close/Moving Avg Price: Latest Price/Moving Average Price
Civmec,2017-7,Price/NTA: Closing Share Price/Net Tangible Assets Per Share (times)
Civmec,2017-7,Relative Price Change [RPC]: Relative price change is price change of stock with respect to Benchmark Index
Civmec,2017-7,"Relative Strength (6 Months): Price close today/Price close 6 months ago, then ranked by percentile within the entire market."
Civmec,2017-7,TSR: Total Shareholder Returns is expressed as an annualized rate of return for shareholders after allowing for capital appreciation and dividend
Civmec,2017-7,Volume Index (VI): Number of shares traded in the period/Average number of shares traded for the period
Civmec,2017-7,Volume Weighted Average Price (VWAP): The Volume Weighted Average Price (VWAP) is the summation of turnover divided by total volume in the same period.

Civmec,2017-7,Annual Return: Dividends Paid In a 12-Month Period/Price at the Beginning of the Period + Capital Gain or Loss over 1 Year/Price 1 Year Ago (%)
Civmec,2017-7,Moving Average Price (n periods): Sum of Prices for each Period/Number of Periods
Civmec,2017-7,Price Close/Moving Avg Price: Latest Price/Moving Average Price
Civmec,2017-7,Price/NTA: Closing Share Price/Net Tangible Assets Per Share (times)
Civmec,2017-7,Relative Price Change [RPC]: Relative price change is price change of stock with respect to Benchmark Index
Civmec,2017-7,"Relative Strength (6 Months): Price close today/Price close 6 months ago, then ranked by percentile within the entire market."
Civmec,2017-7,TSR: Total Shareholder Returns is expressed as an annualized rate of return for shareholders after allowing for capital appreciation and dividend
Civmec,2017-7,Volume Index (VI): Number of shares traded in the period/Average number of shares traded for the period
Civmec,2017-7,Volume Weighted Average Price (VWAP): The Volume Weighted Average Price (VWAP) is the summation of turnover divided by total volume in the same period.
Civmec,2017-7,"Data for the BuySellSignals algorithms is drawn from annual reports, company websites and similar sources of publicly available data. It should be used as a guide only."
